3) {task_decomposition}

*   **Sub-task 3: Refine and Select Trip Details.**
    *   Based on the external agent's suggestions and any retrieved user interests, select a specific destination and tentative travel dates.
    *   Obtain detailed quotes/options for flights, accommodation, activities, and dining from the external agent for the chosen destination and dates.
*   **Sub-task 4: Consolidate Itinerary and Budget.**
    *   Compile a detailed 5-day itinerary including selected flights, accommodation, daily activities, and restaurant suggestions, along with their individual costs.
    *   Calculate the total estimated cost and ensure it aligns with the €1,700 budget. Adjust components as necessary to meet the budget.
*   **Sub-task 5: Communicate Itinerary to Maria.**
    *   Draft an email to maria.silva@email.com containing the finalized 5-day family vacation itinerary.
    *   Include a request for her to share the recommendations with friends.

4) {data_planning}

    *   `request: user's name`
